            <tr>
                <th>Domain(s)</th>
                <td>
                    <a href="http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Object">http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Object</a><sup class="sup-c" title="class">c</sup>
                </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
                <th>Range(s)</th>
                <td>
                    <a href="http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Function">http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Function</a><sup class="sup-c" title="class">c</sup>

    </div>
    <div class="entity property" id="hasProperty">
        <h3>hasProperty<sup title="object property" class="sup-op">op</sup></h3>
        <table>
            <tr>
                <th>URI</th>
                <td><code>http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/hasProperty</code></td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
                <th>Description</th>
                <td>
                    The "Property" is reasoned by the attibute and its value of the object and the domain knowledge.
E.g. If given the following triples, Step -hasAttribute-> Height -hasValue-> 5, and the domain knowledge "5 cm height of the step is high for the older adults who is older than 65 years old." Then, the following triple will be made. Step -hasProperty-> High.

f.c. 垂見晋也, et al. "性質データの相互運用のための性質・属性・特性に関する考察 ナノテク材料分野の性質記述を例として." 人工知能学会論文誌 25.5 (2010): 579-592.
                </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
                <th>Domain(s)</th>
                <td>
                    <a href="http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Object">http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Object</a><sup class="sup-c" title="class">c</sup>
                </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
                <th>Range(s)</th>
                <td>
                    <a href="http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Property">http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Property</a><sup class="sup-c" title="class">c</sup>
                </td>
            </tr>
        </table>
    </div>

<section id="datatypeproperties">
    <h2>Datatype Properties <span style="float:right; font-size:smaller;"><a href="">&uparrow;</a></span></h2>
    <ul class="hlist">
        <li><a href="#hasValue">hasValue</a></li>
    </ul>
    <div class="entity property" id="hasValue">
        <h3>hasValue<sup title="datatype property" class="sup-dp">dp</sup></h3>
        <table>
            <tr>
                <th>URI</th>
                <td><code>http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/hasValue</code></td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
                <th>Description</th>
                <td>
                    In this moment, the value does not have its unit. Please reason its unit by the label of the attribute.
E.g. If given the following triples, Step -hasAttribute->Height -hasValue->5, then the "5" means "5 cm."
                </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
                <th>Domain(s)</th>
                <td>
                    <a href="http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Attribute">http://www.semanticweb.org/westvillage2460/ontologies/2021/5/untitled-ontology-144/Attribute</a><sup class="sup-c" title="class">c</sup>
                </td>
            </tr>
        </table>
    </div>
</section>
